module rect0_wieght_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[11:0]	addr,
	output reg	[14:0]	q    // x y w h 5bit*4
	);
	reg					[14:0]	rom [4095:0];
	//always @(posedge clk) q <= rom[addr];
	always @(posedge clk) q <= -4096;


endmodule

module weak_thresh_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[11:0]	addr,
	output reg	[12:0]	q    // x y w h 5bit*4
	);
	(* rom_style = "block", ramstyle = "block" *)
	always @(posedge clk) begin
		case(addr)
			0: q <= -129;
			1: q <= 50;
			2: q <= 89;
			3: q <= 23;
			4: q <= 61;
			5: q <= 407;
			6: q <= 11;
			7: q <= -77;
			8: q <= 24;
			9: q <= -86;
			10: q <= 83;
			11: q <= 87;
			12: q <= 375;
			13: q <= 148;
			14: q <= -78;
			15: q <= 33;

module left_tree_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[11:0]	addr,
	output reg	[13:0]	q    // x y w h 5bit*4
	);
	(* rom_style = "block", ramstyle = "block" *)
	always @(posedge clk) begin
		case(addr)
			0: q <= 534;
			1: q <= -477;
			2: q <= -386;
			3: q <= -223;
			4: q <= -199;
			5: q <= 142;
			6: q <= -432;
			7: q <= -378;
			8: q <= -219;
			9: q <= 318;
			10: q <= -414;
			11: q <= -497;
			12: q <= -142;

module right_tree_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[11:0]	addr,
	output reg	[13:0]	q    // x y w h 5bit*4
	);
	(* rom_style = "block", ramstyle = "block" *)
	always @(posedge clk) begin
		case(addr)
			0: q <= -567;

module strong_thresh_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[4:0]	addr,
	output	reg	[11:0]	q
	);
	(* rom_style = "block", ramstyle = "block" *)
	always @(posedge clk) begin
		case(addr)
			0: q <= -1290 *0.4  ;
			1: q <= -1275 *0.4  ;
			2: q <= -1191 *0.4  ;
			3: q <= -1140 *0.4  ;
			4: q <= -1122 *0.4  ;
			5: q <= -1057 *0.4  ;
			6: q <= -1029 *0.4  ;
			7: q <= -994  *0.4  ;
			8: q <= -983  *0.4  ;
			9: q <= -933  *0.4  ;
			10: q <= -990  *0.4  ;
			11: q <= -951  *0.4  ;
			12: q <= -912  *0.4  ;
			13: q <= -947  *0.4  ;
			14: q <= -877  *0.4  ;
			15: q <= -899  *0.4  ;
			16: q <= -920  *0.4  ;
			17: q <= -868  *0.4  ;
			18: q <= -829  *0.4  ;
			19: q <= -821  *0.4  ;
			20: q <= -839  *0.4  ;
			21: q <= -849  *0.4  ;
			22: q <= -833  *0.4  ;
			23: q <= -862  *0.4  ;
			24: q <= -766  *0.4  ;
			default: q <= 0;
		endcase
	end
endmodule
module weak_stages_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[4:0]	addr,
	output reg	[7:0]	q
	);
	(* rom_style = "block", ramstyle = "block" *)
	always @(posedge clk) begin
		case(addr)
			0: q <= 8'd9 ;
			1: q <= 8'd16 ;
			2: q <= 8'd27 ;
			3: q <= 8'd32 ;
			4: q <= 8'd52 ;
			5: q <= 8'd53 ;
			6: q <= 8'd62 ;
			7: q <= 8'd72 ;
			8: q <= 8'd83 ;
			9: q <= 8'd91 ;
			10: q <= 8'd99 ;
			11: q <= 8'd115;
			12: q <= 8'd127;
			13: q <= 8'd135;
			14: q <= 8'd136;
			15: q <= 8'd137;
			16: q <= 8'd159;
			17: q <= 8'd155;
			18: q <= 8'd169;
			19: q <= 8'd196;
			20: q <= 8'd197;
			21: q <= 8'd181;
			22: q <= 8'd199;
			23: q <= 8'd211;
			24: q <= 8'd200;
			25: q <= 8'd0;
			26: q <= 8'd0;
			27: q <= 8'd0;
			28: q <= 8'd0;
			29: q <= 8'd0;
			30: q <= 8'd0;
			31: q <= 8'd0;
			default: q <= 0;
		endcase
	end
endmodule
module weak_stages_acc_rom(
	input 				clk,
	input		[4:0]	addr,
	output reg	[11:0]	q
	);
	(* rom_style = "block", ramstyle = "block" *)
	always @(posedge clk) begin
		case(addr)
			0: q <= 9	;
			1: q <= 25  ;
			2: q <= 52  ;
			3: q <= 84  ;
			4: q <= 136 ;
			5: q <= 189 ;
			6: q <= 251 ;
			7: q <= 323 ;
			8: q <= 406 ;
			9: q <= 497 ;
			10: q <= 596 ;
			11: q <= 711 ;
			12: q <= 838 ;
			13: q <= 973 ;
			14: q <= 1109;
			15: q <= 1246;
			16: q <= 1405;
			17: q <= 1560;
			18: q <= 1729;
			19: q <= 1925;
			20: q <= 2122;
			21: q <= 2303;
			22: q <= 2502;
			23: q <= 2713;
			24: q <= 2913;
			25: q <= 2913;
			26: q <= 2913;
			27: q <= 2913;
			28: q <= 2913;
			29: q <= 2913;
			30: q <= 2913;
			31: q <= 2913;
			default: q <= 0;
		endcase
	end
endmodule
